(21st)

Another Strike Wave Breaks Out at the Kailuan Coal Mines

Clash Between Workers and Police, Three Workers Shot Dead

Hebei Provincial Government Orders Strict Suppression

Tianjin Correspondence: The Kailuan Coal Mines include six mining areas such as Tangshan, Majiagou, Linxi, and Guye, with tens of thousands of workers. The coal produced annually supplies factories in North China and is worth tens of millions of yuan, making it one of the largest foreign-owned enterprises in China. The mining areas are all located in various counties in the Luan River area. The composition of the workers is complex. After the war zone was recovered last year, traitors and communists have been trying to agitate the workers in an attempt to disrupt the local area. In March of this year, there were two labor strikes, which were fortunately resolved by the authorities without incident. Unexpectedly, the Tangshan mining area had unstable news the other day (18th). The Tangshan Public Security Bureau received the news that there were about five or six thousand workers in the Tangshan mining area and feared that it would cause another incident. That afternoon, it summoned workers' representatives Zhang and Ma for questioning and intended to persuade them. The workers mistakenly thought that Zhang and Ma were arrested, so they gathered hundreds of people and surrounded the Public Security Bureau. The bureau then released the workers who had been summoned. In the evening, the workers went on strike. The next morning (19th), many workers guarded the mine entrances, preventing other workers from going to work. At that time, there were still more than 200 workers and four foreigners underground. They threw bricks and stones from above, intending to cause danger. At the same time, other workers used flammable materials to burn the wood piled up in the mine. Seeing the serious situation, the Public Security Bureau sent police to suppress them. The workers refused to obey and a conflict broke out. The workers attacked with wooden sticks, and the security team had no choice but to open fire as a warning. As a result, three workers, Hu Zhenhai and Yang, etc., were killed, and Du Shun, Wu Yusheng, Hu Baochao, Zhao Wanshun, etc., were seriously injured. Stray bullets injured one peddler and one foreign overseer, all of whom were sent to the Chinese hospital for treatment. On the police side, three people including Wang Huanrong were seriously injured. Martial law has now been declared within the Tangshan mining area, and the situation is still serious today. The provincial government received a telegram from Zhao Xun, Director of the Tangshan Public Security Bureau, and Li Yinchun, the inspector stationed at the factory, yesterday morning reporting the incident. It urgently telegraphed the Tangshan Public Security Bureau: (1) Strictly suppress unstable workers to prevent the situation from escalating; (2) Declare to foreigners that it is absolutely responsible for protecting the property of the mining area. The Department of Industry also simultaneously urged Administrative Inspector Tao Shangming to return to Tangshan to coordinate with the inspector stationed at the factory for a quick settlement. It is reported that the workers' demands include three items: (1) Increase wages; (2) Pay 40 days of fright money; (3) Pay workers' labor money. The above three items are not only outside the previous labor-management agreement, but also the names such as fright money are unheard of. Therefore, all parties believe that there may be another background. (March 20th)

Part of Liu's Bandits Flee into Yucheng, Shandong Province

Ma Brigade Opens Wen Shang to Increase Defense

Jinan Correspondence: Liu Guitang has now fled from Henan to the Caoxian and Dingtao areas of Shandong Province. Yesterday morning, the cavalry regiment had a brief contact with the bandits in the Weiwanji area southwest of Caoxian and drove the bandits back in a panic. Today (20th), it was reported that a part of them fled to the Yucheng county area. In order to strictly prevent them from being completely eliminated, Han specially transferred a part of Ma Guan's 222nd Brigade of the 74th Division stationed in Dezhou to Nankai to strengthen the troops. Ma was receiving training in Jinan and returned to Dezhou last night. He led his troops on three trains and passed Jinan at 6:00 AM today (20th) and planned to disembark at Dawenkou and open Wen Shang for preparation. At the same time, he ordered Dai Hongbin, commander of the armored vehicle, to lead the first armored vehicle team to Yanzhou this afternoon. Jiangxi-Hubei Railway to Start Construction Before June

Scheduled to Be Completed in Three Years

Survey of Profits and Losses of Various Industries in Yuci, Shanxi Province Last Year

More Than 250 Companies Closed Down

Economic Decline, the Market Is Very Depressed

Yuci Correspondence: Since the Spring Festival, news of business closures has been heard every day. The reporter went to the Chamber of Commerce to investigate. Recently, a total of 164 companies have closed down in urban areas and 94 in rural areas, so the market is very depressed. The profit and loss situation of the existing companies last year and the circumstances of the companies that closed down are listed below.

Textile and Electrical Industry (1) Jinhua Textile Factory is the largest factory in Yuci, with a capital of 4 million yuan. Its business losses for the year ending in September totaled more than 370,000 yuan. From October to the end of the year, yarn sales gradually improved, and more than 40,000 packages of cotton were purchased at low prices. Therefore, it made a profit of 100,000 yuan in three months. It was decided at the board meeting on the 7th of this month to still issue half of the official interest of 4%. The shareholders' meeting will be held on April 29th. (2) Weiyu Electric Power Plant is also one of the large-scale enterprises in Yuci, with a capital of 100,000 yuan. Due to high expenses, its surplus last year was 10,000 yuan, and no official interest was paid. The bonus was only about 5%. In addition, too many companies closed down this year, the number of users has decreased sharply, and business is not prosperous. The shareholders' meeting has now entrusted the directors and managers to discuss maintenance methods.

Banking Industry There are 24 money shops and banks here. Thirteen have reported closures, including Jinxilong, Jinshenheng, Yongquantai, Guangyilong, Jinchuan, Jinfengji, Yongxingtai, Deyifeng, Jusheng, Dale Yu, Guangquanqing, Jiyichang, and Yuansheng, with a total capital of more than 400,000 yuan. Others that need to be cleared due to losses are not included. Currently, there are only 11 left, including Jinxin, Zhengxinyu, Yijude, Yuyuanyong, and Wanliheng. Except for Jinxin Zhuang, which made a profit of more than 8,000 yuan, Zhengxinyu, which made more than 6,000 yuan, Yixiangde, which made more than 5,000 yuan, and Yuyuanyong, which made more than 4,000 yuan, the rest can only maintain expenses. The reasons for the losses in the banking industry are approximately twofold: (1) greed for high-interest loans in rural areas; (2) the market's financial resources are exhausted, and turnover is not flexible, which has a great impact.

Color Silk Industry Due to the large inventory and falling selling prices in the color silk industry, 9 out of 20 companies have closed down, including Yongtaiwei, Siyixing, Dejuheng, Yifengtai, Qianyuanji, Ganshengyu, Jilüxin, Yihenghe, and Jinshengji. Moreover, the majority are famous companies with large capital that have been around for a long time. The total capital of each company is about more than 300,000 yuan, with more than 100,000 yuan in debt. The shareholders are at a loss. Only 11 remain, including Yuanjisheng and Ruiningxia. Except for Ruiningxia, which still makes a profit of 5,000 to 6,000 yuan at its external store in Liangzhou, etc., it is rare to find companies that can support themselves.

Calico Industry This industry has declined due to the sharp drop in freight rates, weak purchasing power in rural areas, and the impact of donations and taxes. The business tax owed by each household is as much as 2,000 to 3,000 yuan. Therefore, out of a total of 17 companies, 12 have closed down, including Lijin Company, Jinshengyong, Ruishengxiang, Jifeng Hou, Liquanmao, Yonghe, Juqingyong, Rongdeyi, Yonghe, Guangyilong, Baohe Hou, and Jifengcheng. Except for Jifenghou and Jifengcheng, the capital of the others is also more than 150,000 yuan. Jintong Flower Store made a profit of about 23,000 yuan due to its strong capital. Xiechengyu also has a slight surplus. In addition to those that can offset expenses, it is already a blessing.

Paint Industry The impact on this industry is roughly the same as that of the calico industry. Out of 41 companies of all sizes, 11 have closed down, including Jinfenghou, Tianshunxing, Cuizhenchang, Wanqingwei, Yongyuhe, Yongshengmao, Yongxingquan, Yongshenghao, Yiyinquan, Jinjuhe, and Maoshenghou. The total capital of the closed-down companies is also about 200,000 yuan. Although there are 30 large and small companies remaining, such as Juxingshun and Gongxingshun, losses are common.

Grain Industry This industry has collapsed because of the sharp drop in grain prices, heavy donations and taxes, and the speculative nature of those engaged in it. Therefore, 12 out of 15 companies have closed down, including Defengli, Jujinchuan, Fushengheng, Heji, Deshengheng, Guangshunyi, Dejuxiang, Qingheheng, Deyusheng, Qingyufeng, Tianyi, and Jinfengzheng. The total capital is also more than 200,000 yuan. Only three companies, including Jitai Gong, remain, and the losses are also significant.

Wine and Noodle Industry The wine industry has been affected by the weak purchasing power of the public and the increase in liquor taxes, while the noodle industry has been affected by the sharp drop in wheat prices and the decrease in business. Therefore, 11 out of 25 companies have closed down, including Deshengyong and Tongquanyong. The capital is also more than 70,000 to 80,000 yuan. Only 14 remain, including Weiyu Flour Mill and Deshunquan. The capital of the flour mill is 140,000 yuan. There is no official interest, and it can only make a profit of more than 12,500 yuan. Most of the smaller capital companies have suffered losses.

Transportation Industry Due to the reduction in freight and the heavy burden, the losses are greater than in other industries. Of the 8 companies in total, 2 have closed down, including Huifengchang and Henglitong. The capital of each is more than 10,000 yuan. The remaining six companies are Yiheyong, Wanfeng, Jitalong, Yishengtong, and Yishenghe. Except for Yiheyong, which still makes a profit by transporting cotton, the others have more losses than profits.

Tobacco Industry Currently, because more people are competing to smoke Jinhua paper cigarettes from this province, and British and American cigarettes are also packaged and sold by Jinhua, Tongji Tobacco Shop, which opened in August and September of last year, closed down this year along with Yonghe Company, Hengyuanhao, Sanyi Tobacco Shop, and Tongji Tobacco Shop. The remaining dry tobacco industry has also been closed because of the small number of sales, and Taichang has also closed with a total of 81. Five of the 12 industries, such as the clothing and cloth industry, tobacco industry, transportation industry, pawnbroking industry, and grain industry, are likely to be unable to establish trade associations due to the lack of the legal number of members. (March 14th)

Recent News on the Training Conference of the First Administrative Region of Jiangxi Province

The current chairman of the Mass Training Committee of the First Administrative Region of Jiangxi Province is Li Jiading. Since its organization and establishment on February 1, it has spared no effort in carrying out mass training work. For example, the cadre training class for the communist eradication volunteer team, the guard teams for bunkers, roads, bridges, and transportation lines in various counties and districts, patrol teams, detective teams, relay posts, and Baojia training have all been organized and completed one after another. Zhang Liangfu, vice chairman of the committee, personally led a large number of trainers and instructors to various districts to conduct strict training. It is expected that results can be achieved in the shortest time. As for other aspects of mass education and relief, such as the establishment of mass fire brigades, mass health associations, health inspection brigades, propaganda teams, mass clinics, vaccination clinics, mass libraries, reading rooms, national martial arts halls, mass schools in urban and rural areas, and the New Life Movement Promotion Association, the committee has vigorously promoted them, donated funds, and gradually organized and established them.

Nanhui

Factory Worker Suspected of Stealing Socks Commits Suicide

A Hu surname sock factory in the Sidun area of the Fourth District of the county was stolen 260 gross of thread socks the day before yesterday. The socks were originally kept by workers Wang Yinxiang, etc. The factory owner Hu Erguan suspected that Yinxiang was heavily involved. Yinxiang asked himself that he had not committed this act, and was unwilling to be wronged, but suffered from not being able to prove it. So he suddenly had the idea of suicide. Last night, he hanged himself in his bedroom. After the factory owner discovered it, he was extremely shocked and immediately reported it to the county government through the district office. It was decided that the investigating judge would be dispatched today (22nd) with the examiner to conduct an autopsy and a thorough investigation of the factory owner and others.

Taicang

Dismantling a Deserted Grave Results in a Crushing Death

Wang A’gen, a farmer living in Shangqi Tu outside the South Gate, hired workers to dismantle an abandoned grave in the field because it occupied a large area of land. However, the grave was unusually strong and took a long time to excavate. On the morning of the 21st, one end of the grave was finally demolished. A’gen then climbed into the hole to carry out work. Because the surrounding ash and sand were loosened during the demolition, the stone slab covering the top fell down, crushing A’gen to death. When the other workers lifted the stone slab, his flesh was blurred and looked like a meat pie, a tragic sight. Yang A’sheng, who entered with A’gen, was also seriously injured and was immediately taken to the hospital for treatment. It is said that his injuries are very serious and his life is in danger.

Wuxi

The Liu Zhuomin Case's Scope Expands

After former Public Security Second Sub-bureau Chief Liu Zhuomin was ordered to be dismissed, because his wife, Li Rongzhen (also known as Wen Rongzhen), had a sworn sister relationship with Li Shuyun, the concubine of Gu Renfa, the Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Jiangsu Province, he hid guns and official seals and refused to hand them over, leading to his being placed under the supervision of the County Public Security Bureau and sent to the court. Liu was temporarily released on a written bail of four hundred yuan, while Li was detained pending investigation. Furthermore, Chen Guofu, the Chairman of Jiangsu Province, investigated and found that Director Gu's concubine, Li Shuyun, and her mother had been engaging in activities such as flaunting their influence to extort money and selling official positions. He reported this to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, who dispatched personnel to arrest Li Shuyun and her mother on Ma Lang Road in Shanghai and hand them over to the Second Special District Court. At the same time, he ordered Magistrate Yan of this county to send a letter to the county court, dispatching bailiffs Yang Shuzi and Feng Yongbao to Shanghai with the letter to escort Li Shuyun and her mother back to the county for interrogation. This matter has already been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the inside story of this case is extremely complex and the situation is becoming increasingly serious. A few days ago, Magistrate Yan received another order from the province, stating that when Liu Zhuomin was in office, he had privately settled cases involving the use of "red pills" (likely referring to opium or similar substances), committed fraud, and engaged in corrupt practices. He was ordered to immediately arrest Liu and hand him over to the law. After receiving the order, Magistrate Yan immediately secretly sent a letter to the Procuratorate of the county court, which dispatched bailiff Huang Yong to Liu's residence in the Donghu Hotel at 10:00 AM yesterday (the 23rd) to arrest him and take him to the court, where he was temporarily detained pending trial. At the same time, he telegraphed the County Public Security Bureau, ordering the Inspector General Zhang Yu, Inspector Liu Renyi, and the newly appointed Second Sub-bureau Chief Gao Lian to go to the court for questioning. In the afternoon at 3:00 PM, Chief Qian opened an investigation court for interrogation. As a result, it was ordered that Liu Zhuomin be taken into custody, and the others were ordered to return. As for Li Shuyun and her mother, they were originally scheduled to be escorted from Shanghai around 12:00 noon yesterday (the 23rd) and arrive in Wuxi around 4:00 PM. However, as of 5:38 PM, when the northbound special express train arrived at the station, Li Shuyun had not been seen being escorted to Wuxi.

Fire Under the Embankment Claims the Life of an Elderly Woman

At Yanxia, near Jiangxi Bridge Town in the Second District, a rural woman named Hua, aged fifty-six, met with misfortune. Last night, the Hua family was careless, and neighbors heard the alarm and sounded gongs to call for help. Fire brigades from nearby rushed to the scene to put out the fire, but it was too late. All two rooms and three sections of the house were reduced to ashes. Hua was unable to escape and perished in the flames, a truly tragic event. The neighboring Chenhua Elementary School building was also affected, but the damage was slight.

Zhenjiang

Request to Exempt Hong Oil from Business Tax

The Tong Oil shops in Zhenjiang argue that the two types of Hongjiang oil and Xiu oil are made from Tong oil raw materials and are sold exclusively domestically. There is no foreign trade. When shipped out of Hongjiang and passing through Hankou, the local Commodity Inspection Bureau also requires them to pay the same inspection fees as Tong oil. The Business Tax Bureau even requires them to pay the same export business tax as Tong oil, which seems to violate the purpose of the state establishing bureaus to collect taxes. Although the oil shops have branches in Hankou, they are solely responsible for handling the transshipment of goods from the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. Small barrels of Hong oil are also among the transshipped goods and there is no business activity involved. Forcing them to pay taxes is no different from levying internal transit duties. They have jointly submitted a request to the Hubei Finance Department, asking it to order the Hankou Business Tax Bureau to exempt the two items of Hong oil and Xiu oil that are transshipped from export business tax to alleviate the difficulties of the merchants.

Luhe

Charity Association Provides Relief to the Poor and Sick

The Poverty Relief Clinic of the Charity Association outside the East Gate of this county has been established for three years and has achieved good results. The Chinese and Western doctors hired are able to conduct thorough research in the area of diagnosis without the slightest negligence. Therefore, dozens of people come to the clinic every day. It is said that those who are extremely poor are not charged any fees. Even those who are not extremely poor are only charged ten copper coins for registration. Western medicine is provided by the association, and Chinese medicine is also provided to the poor and sick by the association. If a sick person from another province or a distant place wants to stay in the association for treatment, they only need to obtain a formal letter of guarantee or a letter from an organization or group, and it is acceptable. Recently, the association also started providing free smallpox vaccinations from the 16th for the general poor and sick. The establishment of the Poverty Relief Clinic of the Charity Association is truly a blessing for the poor and sick. However, it is heard that the association is facing financial difficulties and plans to raise funds. It is thought that there is no shortage of charitable people in this county who will provide generous assistance.

Kong Xiangxi Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning to Discuss Unifying National Finances

National Finance Conference to be Held in Mid-June

Kong and Song Will Go to Nanjing on the 25th to Attend the Economic Conference

Kong Xiangxi, the Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, arrived in Shanghai by night train from Nanjing at 7:25 AM yesterday. He went straight to his private residence on West Yanan Road to rest. He then met with reporters from various newspapers around 10 AM. At noon, he went to the Central Bank to work. Kong is scheduled to go to Nanjing with Song Ziwen, a standing member of the National Economic Council, on the 25th to attend the plenary meeting of the Economic Council. The following is a record of Kong's remarks:

National Finance Conference to be Held in June According to Kong, the Ministry of Finance is scheduled to convene a National Finance Conference in Nanjing in mid-June, inviting finance officials from various provinces to discuss issues such as unifying national finances, abolishing excessive taxes and levies, and reorganizing national land taxes. The Ministry of Finance has decided that in the future, county budgets will be approved by the provincial government, and any shortfall will be subsidized by the provincial government. Provincial budgets will be approved by the central government, and any shortfall will be subsidized by the central government. Only in this way can the goal of unifying national finances and abolishing excessive taxes and levies be achieved. As for the rumors that the National Finance Conference will be held in mid-May, they are not accurate.

Chiang Will Not Attend the Plenary Meeting of the Economic Council Kong continued to say that the National Economic Council is scheduled to convene a plenary meeting in Nanjing on the 26th of this month. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is busy with military operations against the bandits and cannot leave Jiangxi. He will probably not be able to return to Nanjing to attend. Madame Chiang Kai-shek (Soong Mei-ling) is currently staying in Shanghai. The report that she came to Shanghai from Nanjing last night (the 22nd) to treat a dental problem is not accurate.

People Along Baoshan Dike Urge Allocation of Funds for Dike Repair

Delay Will Have Unforeseen Consequences

Yan Fenglou and others, dike directors along the Baoshan Dike, telegraphed: Nanjing National Economic Council, In recent years, the Jiangnan seawall has not been repaired for a long time, and dangerous situations are emerging one after another. The Baoshan section is particularly important. It suffered two typhoons last year, destroying more than 2,800 zhang. Although the provincial government allocated 60,000 yuan for temporary repairs, there are still many holes and a crisis is looming. If it is not fundamentally repaired, it will not be able to withstand an autumn flood. Last winter, your council sent a foreign engineer to inspect and assess the dike, but several months have passed and construction has not yet started. The people along the coast are extremely anxious. Now that the spring flood season has arrived, we feel even more uneasy. If it is delayed any longer, it will become irreversible. The severity of the disaster may be even greater than the floods in Hankou and Gaoyou in the past or the Yellow River breach last year. Fenglou and others have witnessed the dangerous situation and cannot sit idly by. We urgently appeal to your council to consider that the Jiangnan seawall is of great importance to the national economy and people's livelihood. Give priority to the urgent matter and quickly allocate large sums of money for construction to eliminate the major disaster. The telegram is extremely urgent. Yan Fenglou, the dike director of Baoshan County, Jiangsu Province, and all the people bow. Sealed.

Wu Yun-chu Establishes Tianli Anhydrous Ammonia Products Factory

Factory Site Selected, Machinery Purchased

Manufacturing Can Begin Next Spring

Division of Labor and Cooperation with the Ministry of Industry's Ammonium Sulfate Plant

Central News Agency: Recently, many newspapers carried an Associated Press dispatch from Seattle stating that the machinery of the Pacific Ammonia Chemical Plant there has been sold by the Hengxin Gunpowder Company to an unknown buyer and will be moved to Shanghai within two weeks. The factory was originally a fertilizer manufacturer, but with slight modifications, it can manufacture gunpowder products. Yesterday, Western newspapers also reported that a local industrialist had ordered machinery from France to use the products of the above machinery to manufacture nitric acid, and that the two are part of the same organization. However, the Associated Press did not know the name of the buyer, and the Hengxin Company refused to elaborate on the sale. The ownership of the nitric acid plant was also not detailed. After the reporter inquired in many ways, it was learned that the two plants belong to the same company, and the Tianchu Monosodium Glutamate Factory is the center. The reporter then visited Wu Yun-chu, the manager of the factory, and the following is what he said:

Operating Motivation According to Wu, most small industries are based on light profits and heavy operations, while basic industries are the opposite. In recent years, the Tianchu Factory has been able to stand on its own, so it is engaged in chemical industries that others believe are not easy to run or are unwilling to run, but which must be run from a national standpoint. It is shouldering this important task and making efforts to move forward. Five years ago, it started the green gas industry and established the Tianyuan Electro Chemical Factory. Now the foundation of the factory is solid, and the second step is to establish an anhydrous ammonia industry factory. The anhydrous ammonia industry actually controls the nation's life and death, because grains, fruits, and vegetables rely on anhydrous ammonia fertilizer to grow, and without nitric acid (one of the most important anhydrous ammonia products), there would be no way to supply national defense needs.

Products Next Spring This factory is named the Tianli Anhydrous Ammonia Products Factory, with a capital of one million yuan, which has already been raised. The machinery has been ordered from the United States and France. These are the two factories mentioned in the Chinese and foreign newspapers in recent days. The machinery ordered from the United States has been shipped and will arrive in Shanghai in about a month to be installed, which will take about five months. At that time, the machinery ordered from France can also be shipped and installed continuously. Therefore, the entire completion will take about seven or eight months, and manufacturing must begin in early spring next year. The factory site has been selected near the Tianyuan Factory in Chenjiadu, west of Shanghai. Because after the January 28th Incident, the city of Zhabei was extremely dilapidated, and the local water and electricity plants were greatly affected. After the Tianli Factory starts operations in the future, it will use more than 50,000 degrees of electricity, which will help the sale of electricity.

Manufacturing Steps The manufacturing of the factory is divided into two steps. The machinery ordered from the United States is to catalyze anhydrous ammonia from the anhydrous ammonia in the air and the hydrogen in the water. The machinery purchased from France is to catalyze nitric acid from anhydrous ammonia and oxygen. It is estimated that the machinery can produce 11 tons of nitric acid per day. However, if it needs to be increased, it can be produced up to twice that amount. The above two products are important raw materials in the industry. However, the factory focuses on the production of nitric acid because it can be used to manufacture fertilizer for enriching the soil. Although the factory and the Ministry of Industry's ammonium sulfate factory are both in the same business of fixed anhydrous ammonia from the air, the factory focuses on producing ammonium sulfate, while this factory focuses on producing nitric acid and nitrates, so they divide the labor and cooperate.

National Products Tycoon Wu Zhihao Hosts a Banquet for Various Circles

Exposes Japanese Conspiracies in the United States

Awakens Compatriots to Use National Products

Wu Zhihao, a local national products tycoon, held a spring banquet at the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Association at 6 PM the day before yesterday to assist the Zhibo (Chicago Exposition) Product Cooperation Association and to organize the North China and Northwest China National Products Exhibition. He invited people from all walks of life who were enthusiastic about national products. Those who attended included Qin Runqing, Zhou Guanhong, Xu Shiying, Zha Mianzhong, Hu Chengxiang, Shen Jiucheng, Xu Xinliu, Wu Zhihe, Wang Xiaolai, the County Magistrate Hu of Fenghua, Wu Zhijian, Wang Yansong, Zhou Fainan, Wu Wenjing, Pei Yunqing, Li Zushen, Zhang Zilian, Yuan Duanfu, Xu Tingzuo, Wang Qiyu, Wen Lanting, Lou Shaobai, Zhu Wenqi, Zhang Shenzhi, Shen Tianxin, He Dekui, Zhuo Yuting, Zhang Xianglin, Xiang Weichen, Xue Dubi, Xue Chunsheng, Xu Caicheng, Sun Meitang, Xu Yongzuo, Cheng Shouchu, Dong Boying, Chen Jicheng, and more than 100 other people. Wu Zhihao reported that since the September 18th Incident, Japan, in order to confuse international public opinion, planned to take advantage of the opportunity for various countries to participate in the Chicago Exposition in the United States to conduct organized and complete propaganda that would damage our country and intended to realize its consistent claim to seize all markets in our country. It spared no expense to lure Chinese traitors to transport a large number of enemy goods and vigorously dump them. This can be known from the monthly customs reports on Japanese goods imports. However, the Japanese are still not satisfied. After encroaching on our four northeastern provinces, they threatened North China and planned to seize Tianjin again and advance into the Northwest and Henan-Shandong provinces. Zhihao and his colleagues, in view of the impending national crisis, felt that if we do not catch up quickly, death will not be far away. Therefore, last year, after the government decided to stop participating in the Zhibo because of the loss of Rehe, the emergency in Tianjin, and the shortage of transportation funds, he appealed to the financial community, Zhang Gongquan, Chen Guangfu, Lin Kanghou, Xu Xinliu, and the industrial community, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, and other gentlemen, to raise funds and present them to the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance, which subsidized 50,000 yuan of national currency to organize the Product Cooperation Association to participate as scheduled. According to the report of the association, the Japanese did hire an American beauty in the Zhibo meeting place to give a lecture, publicly insulting our national integrity and deliberately making various counter-propaganda. They placed our old and worst products in the same place as their newest goods and drove the public to watch. Later, the Chinese Pavilion used various methods to strongly negotiate with the Zhibo, and the conference officially sent a letter to prohibit it. Finally, the Japanese side was angry and sold off the beauty and threatened the Zhang representative of the pavilion with a gun. From this one incident, we can know the ambition of the Japanese. Therefore, the value of this trip is not only to expose the Japanese conspiracy and obtain the good sympathy and praise of the Europeans and Americans, but also to enhance the international position and create a foundation for foreign trade. The Zhibo has decided to continue the exhibition for another year. The colleagues will continue to assist the association in taking a step further. For the fundamental plan to promote national production, they have obtained the government's strong assistance and have been unanimously initiated and supported by all walks of life in the country to organize the China National Product Production and Sales Joint Company in Shanghai, with the hope of establishing branches across the country and creating a large group of production, sales, talent, and economy. In addition to handling the work that should be done, the company is also concerned that the Japanese are eyeing North China and that enemy goods are filling the Northwest. In the late winter and early spring of last year, it successively sent letters to the Tianjin and Gansu provincial governments and authorities from all walks of life to agree to organize a large-scale national products exhibition to awaken the people to use national products to build an economic network and serve as a barrier for the northeastern and northwestern provinces. However, the above three matters are of great importance and cannot be fully accomplished without collective efforts. Therefore, today, Zhihao has prepared a simple meal and respectfully invites all of you to attend. I sincerely hope that you will uphold the principle that everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the country and strive to assist together. Zhihao is not talented, but he should follow the骥尾 (refers to following a great person, here meaning to be inspired) and provide inspiration. The words were profound, and the entire audience was moved. Zhou Guanhong, Shen Jiucheng, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Li Zushen, Zhang Zilian, and others then gave speeches. At the end, there was a fun drama by the female staff of the Shanghai National Products Company, Ren Chaojun's flower boxing, the Song of Hate by the singer of the Xifan Film Company, and the scenes of the Zhibo's entire day and night, to entertain the audience. It was not until 11 o'clock that the banquet ended happily.

Guests Welcomed at the Jade Buddha Temple

Wu Peifu, Bai Chongxi, Huang Xuchu, Feng Yuxiang, and Chen Diaoyuan also sent representatives. The carriages and horses filled the door, making it a grand occasion for a time. According to Duan's aides, Duan has no intention of going to Hangzhou for the time being. The rumor that he will go to Hangzhou at the end of the month to participate in the Kalachakra Dharma Assembly is not true.

China National Aviation Corporation and China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Sign Sea-Air Intermodal Transport Contract

Nine Articles of the Contract Officially Signed

The Issue of Ticket Refunds Still Needs to be Considered

Since the Ministry of Railways and the shipping companies signed a land-sea intermodal transport contract, the national intermodal transport will soon be completed. Now, the Ministry of Transportation is further expanding intermodal transport with various foreign airlines. At the same time, sea-air intermodal transport is also being implemented by the local China National Aviation Corporation and the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which are negotiating a sea-air intermodal transport contract. The situation is recorded as follows:

Nine Articles of the Contract China National Aviation Corporation and China Merchants Steam Navigation Company recently noted that the number of passengers transferring from ships to airplanes is increasing, and the number of passengers transferring from airlines to ships to reach ports not yet reached by air is also increasing from time to time. In order to facilitate passengers, it has been decided to implement sea-air intermodal transport. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company can issue joint tickets for passengers who want to transfer to airplanes, and vice versa, airlines can also sell China Merchants Steam Navigation Company ship joint tickets for passengers who want to transfer to the merchant ships. The two parties have convened multiple negotiations on the joint transport contract. After repeated deliberation and revision by both the airline and the shipping company, nine articles of the sea-air intermodal transport contract have been officially signed.

Immediate Implementation Regarding sea-air intermodal transport, each will use its existing routes as the scope. China National Aviation Corporation's current aircraft have the Shanghai-Chengdu line (which can be connected with ships along the Yangtze River), the Shanghai-Peiping line (which can be connected with ships in the Bohai Sea), and the Shanghai-Guangdong line (which can be connected with ships in the South China Sea). All places that can be reached by the ships and airplanes of the two airline and shipping companies are places where intermodal transport tickets can be mutually sold. The procedures are very simple and convenient for passengers. Currently, only the issue of ticket refunds still needs to be considered. After the two parties have prepared the formal contract and exchanged it, intermodal transport can be implemented.

Construction of Docks and Opening of Shipping Routes in Sanmen Bay

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to Proceed in Two Steps

The development of Sanmen Bay is actively underway with overseas Chinese investing capital. It has been decided that an inspection group will be organized on April 1st. The construction of docks and opening of shipping routes by the China Merchants Bureau has also been agreed upon and will be carried out in two phases. Recent news is reported as follows:

Overseas Chinese Investment: Recently, many overseas Chinese from various regions have invested in claiming nearby open land in Sanmen Bay. The price of land is very low, but due to the large number of purchasers, it has gradually increased. As of now, the land claimed by overseas Chinese in Sanmen Bay has reached more than 3,000 acres. Most of the land claimed is in the Jianba area. The large landowners, such as Liang Sheng, have now organized the Jianba Area Land Claim Committee.

Scheduled Inspection: For the purpose of assisting in the development of Sanmen Bay, the Jianba Area landowners have organized the Overseas Chinese Sanmen Bay Inspection Group. They have now gathered overseas Chinese to form a group and are scheduled to go to Sanmen Bay on April 1st to conduct on-site inspections and study the opening of the port and the development of various industries in the area. Investors hope that the authorities will expedite the two major issues of port construction and navigation, so that the Sanmen Bay market will flourish, land prices will increase, and the goal of establishment will be gradually achieved.

Request for Port Construction: The Jianba Area Land Claim Committee has recently submitted a request to the Ministry of Communications, stating that Banba and Jiangdong Port in Sanmen Bay are natural seaports and transportation hubs, and essential areas for reaching various parts of Zhejiang. Construction in Sanmen Bay should begin with the construction of docks in these two locations. They specifically request the Ministry of Communications, from a national standpoint, to order the China Merchants Bureau to quickly build wharves in Jiangdong Port and Banba as the foundation for opening Sanmen Bay, and to open shipping routes in the short term, so that cargo transportation in eastern Zhejiang can be shipped from there.

Ministry of Communications Solicitation: Based on the submission from the Jianba Area Committee, which invested in land purchases, the Ministry of Communications immediately instructed the state-owned China Merchants Bureau to solicit opinions regarding the construction of Banba and Jiangdong Port wharves in Sanmen Bay, as well as the addition of shipping routes from Sanmen Bay to various locations. They were ordered to submit their opinions immediately. After receiving the order, the China Merchants Bureau submitted the matter to the Business and Shipping Departments. The result of the discussion was that the construction of Banba and Jiangdong Port wharves and the opening of shipping routes must be carried out in two steps. The first step is to build Jiangdong Port wharves and warehouses when Sanmen Bay has a port model and a commercial market begins. When cargo transportation is secure, new shipping routes will be opened. The report was submitted to the Ministry of Communications for review yesterday.

Wu Tianmin Discusses the Recent Situation in the Northeast

All Industries are Monopolized by the Japanese

The People of the Northeast are Complaining Endlessly

Every Day They Hope for the Central Government to Recover the Lost Territory

Actively Laying Railroads to Facilitate Military Affairs

New News Agency reports that since the "September 18th Incident," the four northeastern provinces have successively fallen. Although there are still some patriotic people continuing to fight the enemy on the border, it is regrettable that the general public seems to have ignored the suffering after the event. Recently, Mr. Wu Tianmin, who returned from the pseudo-state, arrived in Shanghai a few days ago and joined the refugee self-help group led by Jiang Minsheng, the "Leather Shoe General," to support himself. According to him, the recent situation in the pseudo-state is quite detailed. The following are the details of his statement:

Implementation of Immigration Policy: Since Pu Yi was used by the Japanese to usurp the throne on March 9, 1932, the Japanese have used this as a deceptive means externally. On the one hand, they implemented an immigration policy, with Koreans accounting for 70% to 80%, and Japanese accounting for only a small number. The areas with the most immigrants are Yilan, Harbin, and Zhaozhou along the Songhua River, followed by the vicinity of Tao Si Zha. Before the September 18th Incident, Japanese already occupied a considerable position in various important cities in the three eastern provinces, regardless of industry or commerce. Therefore, the monopoly of industry and commerce after the recent immigration is self-evident.

Recovering Lost Territory in the Northeast: After the Japanese occupied the area, they used deceptive means to try to lure the people, but their ferocious face was finally revealed. The people felt that they were being manipulated by the Japanese everywhere, making it difficult to make a living. Usually, when minor disputes occurred with the Japanese, they were bound to suffer. Therefore, the people there are complaining endlessly and hope that the central government will recover the lost territory in the Northeast as soon as possible.

Confiscating Firearms from the Public: Most of the people there have self-defense firearms, because of the frequent bandits. Recently, the Japanese secretly feared that the people would take the opportunity to revolt. In areas close to cities, they have confiscated firearms from house to house. Those far from the city have requested the Japanese military to postpone the confiscation in order to defend against bandits. The Japanese feared that being too strict might cause misfortune, so they have temporarily agreed. It is expected that the confiscation will be completed soon.

Korean Army Supervising the Puppet Army: The troops compiled by the puppet state, nominally called brigades, are actually less than two regiments. The organization of each regiment has only two people serving as advisors or counselors in the regimental headquarters (the divisions and brigades increase proportionally). Although their titles seem empty, the highest-ranking officers must be commanded by the advisors or counselors when dealing with any affairs. Therefore, the entire puppet army is controlled by the Japanese and cannot exercise freedom. Recently, the Japanese, fearing that the puppet army stationed in northern Hebei would rebel, have increased the deployment of the Korean army to supervise them, to prevent accidents. This shows a glimpse of the psychology of the puppet army.

Actively Laying Railroads: Since the Japanese occupied the four northeastern provinces, they have been actively laying railroads to facilitate military transportation, as buying out the Chinese Eastern Railway has been difficult. The completed ones include the Jiha Railway (from Jilin to Harbin, about 500 li long), the Jihui Railway (from Dunhua to Tianbaoshan, already connected), the Jitong Railway (from Jilin to Tongjiang, about 1,200 li long), and the Angchang Railway (from Angangxi to Changchun, about 800 li long). The remaining ones that are not yet completed but are planned include the Taoan to Lubei Railway, which is about 1,800 li long.

Shanghai Manufacturers in Panic Over Trademark Argument That Only Considers Shape, Not Sound

Believe the Judicial Yuan's Interpretation is Far From Reality

Trademark Disputes Will Become More Frequent

The Far East News Agency reports that regarding the provision in Article 1, Paragraph 2 of the Trademark Law, which stipulates that the words, graphics, symbols, or combinations used in a trademark must be particularly distinctive, the interpretation by the Judicial Yuan that the words in the Trademark Law only refer to the shape they express and do not include pronunciation has caused panic among manufacturers in Shanghai. They believe that this will make it easier for others to counterfeit their brands. The following is a record of the process of this interpretation and the opinions of manufacturers:

Two Different Opinions: Previously, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce had two different interpretations regarding whether the term "literature" in the provision included pronunciation. Opinion A stated that ordinary philology is divided into three categories: shape, sound, and meaning. Should pronunciation, which is sound, be included? Opinion B stated that trademarks are a type of mark. Referring to the conditions of similarity or approximation listed in Article 2 of this law, such as national seals, military flags, official seals, medals, party flags, party emblems, portraits, names, awards, commendations, and business names, all of which are concrete marks and have nothing to do with sound, pronunciation should not be included. Both opinions had their reasons. Also, if pronunciation is included, China has a vast territory and complex dialects, but the sale of goods should be nationwide. If problems of similar pronunciation occur without standards, there will be numerous disputes. Which pronunciation should be used as the basis?

Original Interpretation: Later, the Ministry submitted the matter to the Executive Yuan for interpretation by the Judicial Yuan. The Judicial Yuan then issued a reply. The original text of the Judicial Yuan's reply was obtained from the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and is transcribed as follows: (Omitted above) This case has been resolved by the Uniform Interpretation of Laws and Regulations Conference of this Court. Article 1, Paragraph 2 of the Trademark Law only states that the words used in a trademark must be particularly distinctive and specifies the color to be used. This shows that the words in the Trademark Law only refer to the shape they express and do not include pronunciation. The meaning is further clarified by the examples in Article 2 of the same law, all of which indicate shape and have nothing to do with pronunciation. A corresponding reply is hereby made.

Manufacturers' Opinions: After reading the above interpretation of the Judicial Yuan, manufacturers in Shanghai were greatly alarmed. According to a powerful manufacturer who spoke to a reporter from the Far East News Agency yesterday, this interpretation by the Judicial Yuan is too far from the reality of manufacturers. Old brands that have been sold for many years will inevitably be counterfeited by unscrupulous merchants. Because national education in our country has not been popularized, there are not many literate people. If the shape of the words is the only consideration for word trademarks, and the pronunciation of the words is not considered, it is tantamount to only looking with the eyes and not listening with the ears. For example, if the products of Factory A use "山羊" (mountain goat) as a trademark, and Factory B sees that the "山羊" products of Factory A are selling very well, they will use "三陽" (three suns) as a trademark and sell similar goods, mixing them in the market. How can illiterate customers distinguish them? It is feared that cases of trademark disputes and lawsuits will be even more frequent in the future.

The Chinese Ratepayers' Association Sent Out Citizen Group Election Tickets Yesterday

A Total of 5,274 Tickets

The 13th election of the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Public Concession, including the investigation procedures and the preparation of the register, has been completed. Yesterday at 2:00 PM, the election tickets for the citizen group were sent out, and various groups were invited to attend the meeting to check the tickets and monitor the issuance of tickets. The details are as follows:

Inspection of Ballots: Yesterday at 2:00 PM, the association sent out 5,274 citizen group election tickets. Representatives from the Bankers Association, including Lin Kanghou; the Money Trade Association, including Wu Rulin; the Citizens' Union, including Zhang Yiqing; the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, including Zhu Wenqi; the Shaoxing-Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association, including Ren Xiangsheng; the Ningbo-Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association, including Mao Heyuan; and the executive committee members Xu Jiqing and Hu Fengxiang attended the meeting to check and monitor the mailing of the tickets. It was also decided that March 27th (Tuesday) from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM will be the ballot checking period, and the ballots will be counted on the 28th at 9:00 AM.

Election Notice: The association issued an election notice yesterday, stating: "Dear Sir/Madam, the qualifications of the electors and candidates for the 13th election of the association have been announced in the newspapers and confirmed. It is now decided that the voting period will be from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM on March 27th. The ballot box will be set up at the Bankers Association downstairs of the association building. The ballots will be counted from 9:00 AM the next morning. We are sending you one election ticket and one list of candidates and ask you to check the election instructions printed on the election ticket. This concerns the exercise of your electoral rights, so please do not give them up. With best wishes."

Investigation Report: The association also released the 3rd election report, stating: "In addition to publishing notices in the newspapers and soliciting taxpayers to come to the association to fill out the forms, as usual, the association also pre-filled the names of taxpayers based on the previous register and then sent staff to conduct investigations in various ways. If there were no changes, the old information was retained, and the taxpayer only needed to stamp the investigation form for verification. If there were changes, a new form was filled out. As of December 25th of last year, a total of 5,436 investigation forms were received. Before the register was prepared, excluding duplicate and unqualified forms, a total of 5,270 investigation forms were actually received. After the investigation was completed, the election register was prepared, distinguishing those with and without voting rights. On March 13th, a public notice was published in the newspaper according to the election regulations. If there were any errors or omissions, taxpayers were asked to come to the association before March 20th to correct or add them. The deadline was considered final. A total of eight people came to the association during the period to declare additions. A total of 5,278 investigation forms were received before and after. Therefore, the draft number of the election register was 5,278 elector names. After the names of electors were entered into the register and draft numbers were assigned, there were still three people who were unqualified due to insufficient tax amount and one person who had passed away. There are still 5,274 people left, including 2,734 people with the right to be elected and 2,540 people with the right to vote. Therefore, the official number is 5,274, and the number of election tickets issued is 5,274, which adds up to the above number. Please refer to the investigation statistics table."

Collection of Joint Transportation Parcel Fees Upon Arrival

To be Implemented from April 1st

The Ministry of Railways, based on the Joint Transportation Office's proposed five articles for the collection of joint transportation parcel fees upon arrival, has decided to implement them from April 1st. Yesterday, it specially instructed the railway bureaus to comply with the order. The original order stated: "It is reported by the Joint Transportation Office that joint transportation of parcels is becoming increasingly developed, and many merchants have requested that fees be collected upon arrival. In response to social needs, five articles for the collection of joint transportation parcel fees upon arrival are proposed for review and approval." "After reviewing the proposed articles, they are considered appropriate and should be approved. It is decided to implement them from April 1st of this year. In addition to issuing separate orders, the relevant articles are hereby copied and issued for compliance and reporting." This order has been forwarded by the railway bureaus to the traffic department for compliance. The articles for the collection of joint transportation parcel fees upon arrival are recorded as follows: (1) The fees for joint transportation parcels may be collected by the arrival station from the receiver of the parcel after the parcel arrives, upon the request of the sender of the parcel. (2) The first, second, and third copies of the receipt for joint transportation parcels with fees collected upon arrival should be printed in red with the words "到付" (to be paid upon arrival) to indicate the difference. (The words "預付" (prepaid) in the receipt should be changed to "到付" (to be paid upon arrival).) (3) The arrival station shall be responsible for collecting the fees for parcels with fees collected upon arrival from the receiver of the parcel. If the receiver of the parcel refuses to pay the fees, the arrival station shall immediately notify the originating station to collect the fees from the sender of the parcel. The parcel may only be delivered to the receiver of the parcel after receiving the notification from the originating station that the fees have been collected. If the fees have not been collected or the notification from the originating station that the fees have been collected has not been received, and the parcel is delivered to the parcel receiver, the arrival route shall be responsible for compensating all uncollected fees. (4) Parcels containing easily perishable items or those with an estimated value lower than the transportation fee and without sufficient guarantees may not be transported according to the method of collecting fees upon arrival. (5) The originating stations that send out parcels with fees collected upon arrival shall create and send delivery parcel insurance policies separately from prepaid parcels and indicate "到付" (to be paid upon arrival) in the remarks column. The arrival stations that receive fees for parcels with fees collected upon arrival shall also send delivery parcel reports separately from prepaid parcels and indicate "到付" (to be paid upon arrival) in the remarks column. The accounting offices of each route shall also send them to the clearing division of the Joint Transportation Office for verification.

Shanghai's New Life Movement

Founders Join Enthusiastically

Central News Agency reports that since the various party, government, transportation, and other circles in Shanghai initiated the preparation of the New Life Movement Promotion Association last week and elected Mayor Wu and others as preparatory members, the preparatory office has been opened at the Maple Bridge Local Autonomy Preparatory Office. In addition to actively carrying out the planned programs and publicity guidelines, they have also sent letters to various circles to solicit names to be listed as founders, and the number has reached more than 300 people. The origin of the association and the names of all the founders are recorded below.

Origin: What is "life"? In short, it is the "living" activity of human beings seeking "survival." The activities of human beings seeking survival can be roughly divided into eight categories: food, clothing, housing, transportation, work, education, entertainment, and communication. Whether in ancient or modern times, whether in China or abroad, all human beings should have these kinds of lives. However, although all human beings have these kinds of lives, because of different times, different environments, different intelligence, and different morality, the spirit and form of their lives cannot be completely the same. Moreover, because of these differences in life, savagery and civilization are distinguished, and poverty and wealth are distinguished. Therefore, those who plan for the country must pay attention to the spirit and form of life and guide it favorably. From this, they create rites and music, establish various principles, and establish various norms to guide the lives of the people. Mr. Sun Yat-sen regarded life as the second element of national composition, and its importance can be imagined. Our country's ancient sages and worthies all paid great attention to their own lives. "The way of university is to illuminate virtue," and its program includes eight items: investigating things, extending knowledge, making the will sincere, rectifying the heart, cultivating the person, regulating the family, governing the state, and pacifying the world. Confucius said, "From the emperor to the common people, all are based on self-cultivation." As for the way of self-cultivation, although there are thousands of strands, they can all be summarized into the principles of "propriety," "righteousness," "integrity," and "shame." If the four words of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame are interpreted in the modern sense, propriety is politeness, righteousness is chivalry, integrity is honesty, and shame is shame. If they are interpreted in the ancient sense, propriety does not exceed the limits, righteousness does not advance itself, integrity does not conceal evil, and shame does not follow injustice. Judging from these two meanings, the righteousness of modern people cannot be abolished, and the righteousness of ancient people is also very important. The lack of politeness is indeed a disease of modern society, and the abandonment of discipline and the destruction of order are even more harmful. The lack of a spirit of righteousness is indeed a cause for concern, and the trend of vain advancement is even more of a source of chaos. As for the discussion of integrity and shame, the growth of corruption actually begins with mutual concealment, and the extinction of a sense of shame is mostly due to mutual imitation. Both the ancient and modern meanings are very relevant to the current malpractices. If we can guide the lives of food, clothing, housing, transportation, work, education, entertainment, communication, etc., with the principles of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame and put them into practice, then it will not only be self-cultivation. What is so difficult about regulating the family and governing the country? This is why the New Life Movement is so valuable. Therefore, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, in view of this, specially advocated the New Life Movement in Nanchang and set "order" and "cleanliness" as the first phase of work, gradually reaching the goals of "education," "cultivation," and "hygiene." His intention is very strong. We are located in Shanghai, a ten-mile foreign field, and deeply feel the boredom of life. With the inspiration of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, we are eager to actively improve and are willing to extend this to others to promote the progress of the New Life Movement. Therefore, our association initiates the New Life Movement as the basic work of revitalizing the nation and building the country. We hope that all our compatriots will participate in this initiative.

Concerning the Arrest of Su's Civil Affairs Director Gu Renfa's Concubine, Li Shuyun, Due to an Important Case

Li and her daughter were apprehended in Xinmin Village with the assistance of the French Concession Police.
